[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA global-buffer-overflow vulnerability has been detected in the curl FTP [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimplementation during fuzzing. The issue occurs in the `ftp_state_mdtm_resp` [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunction at `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mftp.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m2107:21[0m[39m`, where an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read operation attempts [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto access memory beyond the bounds of the global variable `Curl_seconds`. This is a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity-critical issue with a SCARINESS score of [0m[1;36m23[0m[39m, indicating a potentially [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexploitable vulnerability.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Vulnerability Type[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is an **AddressSanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39mASAN[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detected global-buffer-overflow** [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability, specifically an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read operation that accesses memory [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately after a global buffer.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Issue Details[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability manifests when the curl_fuzzer_ftp fuzzer processes a test case, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggering the following sequence of events:[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Memory Access Violation**: An [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read operation occurs at address [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x560a67602240[0m[39m`, which is located [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m bytes after the global variable `Curl_seconds`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mdefined in `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mparsedate.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m113[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The `Curl_seconds` variable has a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize of [0m[1;36m480[0m[39m bytes, ending at the exact address where the overflow read occurs.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Call Stack**: The vulnerability is triggered through the following execution [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpath:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The fuzzer entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m initiates a test[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `fuzz_handle_transfer` processes the FTP transfer[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `curl_multi_perform` executes the multi-handle operations[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `multi_runsingle` and `protocol_doing` manage the protocol state machine[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `ftp_doing` and `ftp_multi_statemach` handle FTP-specific operations[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `Curl_pp_statemach` manages the pingpong state machine[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `ftp_statemachine` processes FTP state transitions[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Finally, `ftp_state_mdtm_resp` attempts the out-of-bounds read at line [0m[1;36m2107[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Layout**: According to the shadow byte dump, the memory region shows:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The `Curl_seconds` global variable occupies addresses from `[0m[1;36m0x560a67602060[0m[39m` to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;36m0x560a67602240[0m[39m`[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The accessed address `[0m[1;36m0x560a67602240[0m[39m` falls into a redzone area [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmarked as [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`f9`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which is protection padding placed after global variables[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This indicates the code is attempting to read beyond the allocated buffer[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Investigation[0m                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo understand the full scope of this vulnerability, the following components should[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Primary Source Location** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mftp.c[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Multi-handle Operations** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mmulti.c[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlib/ftp.[0m[1;92mc:2008[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2025[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2008[0m[39m:static bool [0m[1;35mftp_213_date[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconst char *p, int *year, int *month, int *day,[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2009[0m[39m:                         int *hour, int *minute, int *second[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2010[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2011[0m[39m:  size_t len = [0m[1;35mstrlen[0m[1;39m([0m[39mp[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2012[0m[39m:  [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen < [0m[1;36m14[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2013[0m[39m:    return FALSE;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2014[0m[39m:  *year = [0m[1;35mtwodigit[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&p[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m * [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m + [0m[1;35mtwodigit[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&p[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2015[0m[39m:  *month = [0m[1;35mtwodigit[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&p[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2016[0m[39m:  *day = [0m[1;35mtwodigit[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&p[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2017[0m[39m:  *hour = [0m[1;35mtwodigit[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&p[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m8[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2018[0m[39m:  *minute = [0m[1;35mtwodigit[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&p[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m10[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2019[0m[39m:  *second = [0m[1;35mtwodigit[0m[1;39m([0m[39m&p[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2020[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2021[0m[39m:  [0m[1;35mif[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m([0m[39m*month > [0m[1;36m12[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*day > [0m[1;36m31[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*hour > [0m[1;36m23[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m || [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*minute > [0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ||[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2022[0m[39m:     [0m[1;39m([0m[39m*second > [0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2023[0m[39m:    return FALSE;[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2024[0m[39m:  return TRUE;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2025[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlib/ftp.[0m[1;92mc:300[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m311[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m300[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m301[0m[39m: * NOTE: back in the old days, we added code in the FTP code that made NOBODY[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m302[0m[39m: * requests on files respond with headers passed to the client/stdout that[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m303[0m[39m: * looked like HTTP ones.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m304[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m305[0m[39m: * This approach is not elegant, it causes confusion and is error-prone. It is[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m306[0m[39m: * subject for removal at the next [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor at least a future[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m soname bump. Until[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m307[0m[39m: * then you can test the effects of the removal by undefining the following[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m308[0m[39m: * define named CURL_FTP_HTTPSTYLE_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39m.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m309[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m310[0m[39m:#define CURL_FTP_HTTPSTYLE_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39m [0m[1;36m1[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m311[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause Identification[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability occurs at `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mftp.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m2107[0m[39m` where [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_sec[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` is accessed without bounds checking. The issue arises [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfrom the following chain of events:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m2092[0m[39m**: The code explicitly sets `[0m[1;35mputenv[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32mTZ[0m[32m=[0m[32mright[0m[32m/UTC"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` to enable leap [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecond awareness[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m2093[0m[39m**: `[0m[1;35mCurl_gmtime[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is called, which can legitimately return `tm_sec [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m= [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m` for leap seconds when using the [0m[32m"right/UTC"[0m[39m timezone[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Line [0m[1;36m2107[0m[39m**: The `tm->tm_sec` value is used as an array index into [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Curl_seconds`, which only has [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m elements [0m[1;39m([0m[39mindices [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Result**: When `tm_sec = [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m`, this causes an [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m-byte read at index [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m, which is[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout of bounds[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe `ftp_213_date` function correctly validates that seconds can be [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m60[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2021[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2022[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and the [0m[32m"right/UTC"[0m[39m timezone is intentionally used to properly handle [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleap seconds. However, the `Curl_seconds` array definition in [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mparsedate.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m113[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m133[0m[39m` only contains [0m[1;36m60[0m[39m elements for seconds [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m59[0m[39m.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Critical Context[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis code is part of the `CURL_FTP_HTTPSTYLE_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39m` legacy feature [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m300[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m310[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhich is:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Explicitly marked as [0m[32m"not elegant, causes confusion and is error-prone"[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- [0m[32m"Subject for removal at the next [0m[32m([0m[32mor at least a future[0m[32m)[0m[32m soname bump"[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The ONLY location in the entire codebase that uses `Curl_seconds` as an array [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindex[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll other timestamp formatting in the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhttp.c, file.c, vtls/gtls.c, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhsts.c, altsvc.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m uses numeric formatting [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`%02d`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for seconds, which is safe and [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdoesn't have this vulnerability.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Primary Fix: Add Bounds Checking with CURLMIN[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: `[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mftp.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m2107[0m[39m`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange line [0m[1;36m2107[0m[39m from:[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCurl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_sec[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCurl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;35mCURLMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtm->tm_sec, [0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale**:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Minimal Change**: This is a one-line fix that preserves all existing [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfunctionality[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Patterns**: The codebase already uses bounds checking for [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tm_wday` at line [0m[1;36m2101[0m[39m: `Curl_wkday[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_wday ? tm->tm_wday-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Uses Existing Macros**: The `CURLMIN` macro is already defined in [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/curl/lib/[0m[95mcurl_setup.h[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m923[0m[39m` and is designed for this purpose[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Graceful Degradation**: For the rare leap second case [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtm_sec = [0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, it will [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutput [0m[32m"fifty-nine"[0m[39m instead of [0m[32m"sixty"[0m[39m, which is an acceptable approximation given [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe legacy/deprecated nature of this feature[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Breaking Changes**: Preserves the exact behavior for all valid seconds [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvalues [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and only affects the edge case of leap seconds[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **No Test Breakage**: Since there are no existing tests for leap seconds in the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFTP HTTPSTYLE_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39m feature, this won't break any tests[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Implementation Details[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix must be applied to the initial codebase at the exact location where the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow occurs. The change is surgical and affects only the array access:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Before**:[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mmsnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheaderbuf, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheaderbuf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[32m"Last-Modified: %s, %02d %s %4d %02d:%02d and %s seconds GMT\r\n"[0m[39m,[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Curl_wkday[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_wday ? tm->tm_wday-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          tm->tm_mday,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Curl_month[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_mon[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          tm->tm_year + [0m[1;36m1900[0m[39m,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          tm->tm_hour,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          tm->tm_min,[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_sec[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m VULNERABLE LINE[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**After**:[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mmsnprintf[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheaderbuf, [0m[1;35msizeof[0m[1;39m([0m[39mheaderbuf[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[32m"Last-Modified: %s, %02d %s %4d %02d:%02d and %s seconds GMT\r\n"[0m[39m,[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Curl_wkday[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_wday ? tm->tm_wday-[0m[1;36m1[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m6[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          tm->tm_mday,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Curl_month[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mtm->tm_mon[0m[1;39m][0m[39m,[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          tm->tm_year + [0m[1;36m1900[0m[39m,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          tm->tm_hour,[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          tm->tm_min,[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          Curl_seconds[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;35mCURLMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtm->tm_sec, [0m[1;36m59[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m FIXED LINE[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Security**: Eliminates the buffer overflow completely by ensuring the array [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindex never exceeds [0m[1;36m59[0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Preservation**: Maintains all existing functionality and logic paths[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Compatibility**: Does not change the behavior for any non-leap-second [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtimestamps[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Simplicity**: One-line change that's easy to verify and maintain[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **No Side Effects**: [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not modify the `Curl_seconds` array itself[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not change the timezone handling[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not affect the date parsing logic[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not modify the `Curl_gmtime` function[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Does not break the fuzzing harness or test infrastructure[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Defensive**: Protects against the edge case while being aware of the feature's[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeprecated status[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Alternative Approaches Considered and Rejected[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Extending the array**: Adding a 61st element [0m[32m"sixty"[0m[39m to `Curl_seconds` would [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwork but is unnecessary infrastructure for a deprecated feature and a rare edge [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcase[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Changing to numeric format**: Using `%02d` and `tm->tm_sec` directly would [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39malign with the rest of the codebase, but would change the output format of a legacy[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeature that some users might depend on[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Removing the feature**: Undefining `CURL_FTP_HTTPSTYLE_[0m[1;33mHEAD[0m[39m` would eliminate [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe vulnerability but could break backward compatibility[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Modifying timezone handling**: Removing `[0m[1;35mputenv[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"[0m[32mTZ[0m[32m=[0m[32mright[0m[32m/UTC"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` would prevent[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleap seconds but would reduce timestamp accuracy for the intended use case[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Side Effect**: For the extremely rare case of a file with a modification time [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat falls exactly on a leap second [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtm_sec = [0m[1;36m60[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the output will say [0m[32m"and [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32mfifty-nine seconds"[0m[39m instead of [0m[32m"and sixty seconds"[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mif such an array element [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisted[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Mitigation**: This is acceptable because:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Leap seconds are extremely rare [0m[1;39m([0m[39monly [0m[1;36m27[0m[39m have occurred since [0m[1;36m1972[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The feature is deprecated and marked for removal[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-second discrepancy in the textual representation is negligible[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The actual `data->info.filetime` value remains accurate; only the textual [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHTTP-style header is affected[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No functional logic depends on this textual representation[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Preservation of Existing Logic[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix preserves:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All date parsing logic in `ftp_213_date` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding leap second validation[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The timezone handling with [0m[32m"right/UTC"[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `Curl_gmtime` conversion[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The HTTP-style header generation feature[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All conditional checks for when to generate the header[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The exact output format for seconds [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m59[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All other array accesses [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCurl_wkday, Curl_month[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
